name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr

info:Stayed in April 2024

posted:Posted April 30, 2024
msg:A hotel with very good value for money for parent-child travel with children under three years old.
The room is clean and spacious, with a super big bed, and the parent-child room is equipped with toys. The staff are very good and respond very promptly.
There are many children's play areas, but they are not big and relatively simple, enough for small babies. There are not many choices in the Chinese restaurant, but the taste is good, the price is not expensive, and the overall cost performance is very high.
The overall environment of the hotel is very good, built on the mountain, and the greening is well done. It takes 20 minutes to walk up the mountain to the castle. The castle is not open, so it is fine to take a pure walk.
I stayed in the hotel for three days and two nights. The first two days were basically spent in the hotel because of strong wind and rain, which was also rich for a one-and-a-half-year-old baby.
The hotel is indeed a bit old, and the facilities are relatively old, especially the toilet faucet in the bathroom is not smooth to use. The children's playground on the first floor has a slight musty smell, and it feels that it is not used frequently. The breakfast variety is relatively simple, and there are not many types of food for babies.
The overall experience is very good.

msg:I looked at the hotels in Jizhou online, and there are only two that I like, Jingji and Yihao. But the location is a bit far from the city, which is okay for those who drive, and it is not friendly to order takeout. I can't order anything.
Jingji has hot springs and diverse water play. The scenery is not as good as Yihao halfway up the mountain.
Yihao's 2.7-meter splicing bed is invincible, and the landscape room can see the reservoir.
The Yihao landscape room I booked has a large room, good scenery, and a large bed. The service is also good, but breakfast needs to be improved. The piano in the lobby is a plus!
In terms of facilities, the partition door between the shower and the toilet in the bathroom is very rubbish, not waterproof, and the toilet side is also flooded when taking a shower. The bathroom and bedroom are separated by a curtain, which is quite simple.
The hotel lobby is on the north side of the halfway up the mountain. It may be a bit confusing to drive up at night. The hotel logo on Yanshan East Street is not illuminated.
The pretty good half-mountain villa area and castle are not well planned, and are only the exterior decoration of the hotel.
During holidays when there are many people, the door to the terrace is closed and you can only go up through the iron steps outside the castle, which is a safety hazard. There is nothing in the castle, only hard decoration and no soft decoration.
When the park was originally planned, the wasteland on the southeast side of the hotel on Yanshan East Street should have been requisitioned. How will people live in the first row of villas after they are put into use? Now it also affects the hotel living experience.
